    function getCookie(n, k) {
        var reg = new RegExp("(^| )" + n + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");
        var arr = document.cookie.match(reg);
        if (arguments.length == 2) {
            if (arr != null) {
                var kArr, kReg = new RegExp("(^| |&)" + k + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
                var c = arr[2];
                var c = c ? c : document.cookie;
                if (kArr = c.match(kReg)) {
                    return unescape(kArr[2].replace(/\+/g, "%20"));
                } else {
                    return "";
                }
            } else {
                return "";
            }
        } else if (arguments.length == 1) {
            if (arr != null) {
                return unescape(arr[2].replace(/\+/g, "%20"));
            } else {
                return "";
            }
        }
    }
    var daRenHeader = {
        show: function () {
            var logonType = getCookie("LoginValidate", "Type");
            if (logonType && logonType.toLowerCase() == "lifedaren") {
                var daRenHeader = document.getElementById("divDaRenHeader");
                var daRenFooter = document.getElementById("divDaRenFooter");
                if (daRenHeader != null) {
                    daRenHeader.setAttribute("style", "display:block");
                }
                if (daRenFooter != null) {
                    daRenFooter.setAttribute("style", "display:block");
                }
            }
        }
    };
    daRenHeader.show();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
if(clientWidth()<1200) {
    var t=document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].className;
    document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].className=t.replace("sw","");
}
function changeSliderImg(lazyLoad){
    var src = clientWidth()>=1200?"srcA":"srcB";
    var imgs = document.getElementsByName("topSliderImg");
    for(var i=0;i<imgs.length;i++){
        var a=imgs[i].getAttribute(src);
        a!=imgs[i].getAttribute("src")&&imgs[i].setAttribute("src",a);
        if(lazyLoad)return;
    }
}
changeSliderImg(true);
</script>
